 Step 2: Check if animation values are actually being used
The logs show animation is starting. But cards don't move vertically. Let me trace the data flow:

AIBrainstormingStage.vue sets:
- cardStartOffset: 100
- cardMidOffset: -300  
- cardEndOffset: -600

These get passed to FloatingIdeaCards as props. Then used in keyframes:
```js
{ opacity: 0, transform: `translate(-50%, ${props.cardStartOffset}px) scale(0.9)` },
{ opacity: 1, transform: 'translate(-50%, 0px) scale(1)', offset: 0.15 },
{ opacity: 1, transform: `translate(-50%, ${props.cardMidOffset}px) scale(0.95)`, offset: 0.7 },
{ opacity: 0, transform: `translate(-50%, ${props.cardEndOffset}px) scale(0.9)` }
```

Wait - the keyframes are defined at component setup time. But they use `props.cardStartOffset` etc. If these are reactive props, are the keyframes reactive? Or are they evaluated once at setup and then frozen?

That could be the issue! The keyframes might be evaluating to the OLD values from before my changes!

 Step 4: Check CSS for conflicting transforms

Let me look at the CSS again. The cards have:
- Class: `absolute left-1/2 top-1/2`
- This positions them at 50% from parent edges
- They need `translate(-50%, -50%)` to truly center

But I removed the inline style. Now there's NO initial transform. So cards will be positioned with their TOP-LEFT corner at the center point (50%, 50%), making them appear off-center to the RIGHT and DOWN.

The animation keyframes start with `translate(-50%, 100px)`, which should:
- Center horizontally (-50% on X)
- Move down 100px from current position (Y)

But wait - if the card's top-left is at 50%, and we translateY(100px), we're moving down. That's not centered vertically.

  Thought 5/12 

 Step 5: The actual problem - translateY needs to account for centering

When a card has `left: 50%; top: 50%;`, its top-left corner is at center.
To center the card itself, we need `translate(-50%, -50%)`.

My keyframes are:
- `translate(-50%, 100px)` - centers horizontally, but 100px from top-left position (not centered vertically!)
- `translate(-50%, 0px)` - centers horizontally, at top-left position (not centered!)
- `translate(-50%, -600px)` - centers horizontally, 600px up from top-left

But I WANT:
- Start: Card centered, then 100px below center
- Mid: Card perfectly centered  
- End: Card centered, then 600px above center

Solution: translateY needs to be `calc(-50% + Ypx)` to account for vertical centering!

Keyframes should be:
- Start: `translate(-50%, calc(-50% + 100px))`
- Mid: `translate(-50%, -50%)`  
- End: `translate(-50%, calc(-50% + -600px))`
